***увязнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́знуть</a> (19277)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязнуть.html>вя́знуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vjáznutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́знуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvjáznutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вязнуть.html>вя́знуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязать.html>увяза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́зла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mašína <b>uvjázla</b> v grjázi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the car (got) stuck in the mud</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get bogged down <i>(in)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́ши</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:увязнуть.html>увя́знуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долга́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po úši <b>uvjáznutʹ</b> v dolgáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be up to the neck in debt</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:увязывавшийся.html>увя́зывавшийся</a> (30732)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязать.html>увяза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uvjazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязывать.html>увя́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uvjázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:увязать.html>увяза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tie up, to pack up, to strap</li>
<li>to coordinate <i>(with)</i>, to harmonize <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to get the agreement <i>(of)</i></li>
<li>to link <i>(to)</i>, to make conditional <i>(on)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угадать.html>угада́вший</a> (3205)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угадать.html>угада́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugadávšij</span>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угадывавший.html>уга́дывавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugádyvavšij</span>)

***угадываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угадываться.html>уга́дываться</a> (8720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угадывать.html>уга́дывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugádyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угадываться.html>уга́дываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugádyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">угада́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be discernible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:темнота.html>темноте́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:угадываться.html>уга́дывался</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:силуэт.html>силуэ́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v temnoté <b>ugádyvalsja</b> siluét bášni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the outline of a tower could be discerned in the dark</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угасать.html>угаса́ть</a> (10616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угаснуть.html>уга́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugásnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угасать.html>угаса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugasátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угаснуть.html>уга́снуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go out, to become extinct
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:костер.html>костёр</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:угасать.html>угаса́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kostjór <b>ugasájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the fire is dying down</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to die away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:угасать.html>угаса́ют</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">síly <b>ugasájut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one's strength is failing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:угаснуть.html>уга́снуть</a> (13090)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гаснуть.html>га́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gásnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угаснуть.html>уга́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugásnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гаснуть.html>га́снуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угасать.html>угаса́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go out, to become extinct</li>
<li>to die away</li></ol>

***углерод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:углерод.html>углеро́д</a> (23729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>у́голь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">úgolʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">coal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-род</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-rod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to give birth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, because coal consists primarily of carbon. Modeled on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кислород.html>кислоро́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kisloród</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водород.html>водоро́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodoród</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углерод.html>углеро́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugleród</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углерод.html>углеро́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углерод.html>углеро́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углерод.html>углеро́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>carbon</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:угловой.html>углово́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uglovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>angular <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to or forming an angle; sharp-cornered</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:угловой.html>углова́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglovája</b> skórostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>angular</b> velocity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> corner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:угловой.html>углово́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удар.html>уда́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglovój</b> udár</i> ― <span class="e-translation">corner kick</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:углубиться.html>углуби́ться</a> (10718)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">углуби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uglubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубиться.html>углуби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uglubítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубляться.html>углубля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deepen, to become deeper</li>
<li>to go deep <i>(into)</i>, to get deeper <i>(into)</i>, to cut <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубиться.html>углуби́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubítʹsja</b> v les</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go far/deep into the forest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to delve deeply <i>(into)</i>, to become absorbed <i>(in)</i>, to study in depth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубиться.html>углуби́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubítʹsja</b> v knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be deep/absorbed in a book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубиться.html>углуби́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́ли</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:подробность.html>подро́бности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubítʹsja</b> v detáli/podróbnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go into (greater) detail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become more profound/acute, to be intensified, to aggravate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чия</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубиться.html>углуби́лись</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">protivoréčija <b>uglubílisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the contradictions became more acute</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">углуби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uglubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:углубление.html>углубле́ние</a> (12309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">углуби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uglubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубление.html>углубле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uglublénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубление.html>углубле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубление.html>углубле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубление.html>углубле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deepening</li>
<li>hollow, depression</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> draught</li>
<li>intensification
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубление.html>углубле́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотрудничество.html>сотру́дничества</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglublénije</b> sotrúdničestva</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">more intensive/profound cooperation</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубление.html>углубле́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ний</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlja <b>uglublénija</b> svoíx znánij</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to extend/broaden one's knowledge</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубленный.html>углублённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uglubljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">углуби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uglubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубленный.html>углублённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uglubljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>deep <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, absorbed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in; of a person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубленный.html>углублённый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воспоминание.html>воспомина́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubljónnyj</b> v vospominánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deep/absorbed in one's memories</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>deep, in-depth, profound <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a study, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубленный.html>углублённое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изучение.html>изуче́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:литература.html>литерату́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubljónnoje</b> izučénije literatúry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in-depth/profound/thorough study of literature</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***углублять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:углублять.html>углубля́ть</a> (28639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">углуби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uglubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углублять.html>углубля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uglubljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">углуби́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deepen</li>
<li>to extend, to intensify
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углублять.html>углубля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubljátʹ</b> svoí znánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to extend one's knowledge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to aggravate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углублять.html>углубля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubljátʹ</b> protivoréčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to aggravate contradictions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***углубляться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:углубляться.html>углубля́ться</a> (14552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углублять.html>углубля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uglubljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубляться.html>углубля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uglubljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углубиться.html>углуби́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deepen, to become deeper</li>
<li>to go deep <i>(into)</i>, to get deeper <i>(into)</i>, to cut <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to delve deeply <i>(into)</i>, to become absorbed <i>(in)</i>, to study in depth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубляться.html>углубля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubljátʹsja</b> v knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be deep/absorbed in a book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:углубляться.html>углубля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́ли</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:подробность.html>подро́бности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uglubljátʹsja</b> v detáli/podróbnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go into (greater) detail</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become more profound/acute, to be intensified, to aggravate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углублять.html>углубля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uglubljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***углядеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:углядеть.html>угляде́ть</a> (12349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gljadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:углядеть.html>угляде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ugljadétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to find while looking intensely or attentively
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:углядеть.html>угляде́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сестра.html>сестру́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>ugljadéla</b> sestrú v tolpé.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She found her sister in the crowd.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to save from the danger by watching
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:углядеть.html>угляде́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сы́ном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перебегать.html>перебега́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́нием</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otéc ne <b>ugljadél</b> za sýnom i tot stal perebegátʹ úlicu s bolʹšim dvižénijem.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The father missed when his son started to run across the busy street.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
